name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior Queen Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Couples
info:9 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 6, 2024
msg:[A Thousand Words Dismantling the Hotel]
[Me and the Hotel] The reason for choosing Hangzhou Qiantang Puyan Hotel this time is simple: it’s cheap! There was no price increase during May Day! When Hanting, All Seasons, and Atour couldn't book a room for up to 500 to 600 yuan, the price of Hangzhou Qiantang Puyan Hotel on May 2nd was only about 400 yuan. I was a platinum member and got a free upgrade. . Although the hotel is in Xiasha, it is only 200 meters away from the Line 1 subway station. It is just across a shopping mall and can go directly to the city center without changing trains. If you don't want to go to the city center, there are three shopping malls near the hotel, which is really okay.
[Tips from check-in to check-out]
1. The hotel has free parking, both above ground and underground.
2. There are 4 elevators in the hotel, but because 2345 has a dining area, you sometimes have to wait.
3. Your face will be scanned when you check in. The face scan is just for the convenience of checking in. You don’t need to bring your room card with you during the whole process.
4. The room does not require a room card to get electricity. It is available when you open the door. However, you need to click "Welcome" to open the door, otherwise some jacks will be out of power. The lady at the front desk did not tell me about this, so I used it at the beginning. Electricity problem
5. I am not an art major, but the overall design style of the hotel is very avant-garde, with a new Chinese style, which is very attractive to young people. There is a lot of information and promotion on the Internet, so I won’t go into it here.
6. Everything is available in the room, including coffee capsules, smart voice, smart toilet, bathtub, etc. However, "Xiaodu" is a little hard of hearing and sometimes has to shout louder.
7. Complain about the TV. There is no prompt to turn off the TV. I have to put the remote control about 20 centimeters in front of the TV and align it to turn it off. As a result, I turned it off in bed for a long time.
8. The bathrobe is very comfortable, and the full-body shower facility is the first time I have seen it, which is very good. Now that we have a bathtub, how about putting an extra wooden board or somewhere in the bathtub for me to use my phone?
9. The socket was out of power, and the maintenance man called was very patient.
10. Let’s complain about the self-service laundry. The hotel has laundry facilities (charged) and self-service (free). The self-service laundry items are not as good as some budget hotels, including the quality of equipment and the type and quality of laundry detergent. Moreover, the self-service washing machine is on 20F. If I don’t Living on 20F, it seems that the regular elevator cannot go up (you can only go to the floor where you check in), so no one reminded me how to get up (I took the employee elevator myself).
11. I have not tried the catering facilities here, so I will not comment on them.
12. All the staff were very gentle. When they gave me the parking ticket when I left, they also reminded me that I must leave within 15 minutes after scanning the code.
13. The coffee cup of the coffee machine is too big. Go and try it. How much coffee can the coffee capsule produce? Do you need such a big coffee cup? It tastes weird to drink
[Final words]
   This is the first time I have stayed at a hotel under the Lichen Hotel Group. Lichen Hotel is backed by Ctrip and has done a good job in digital operations. I feel very good about this stay, but what is the digital operation behind it, including the hotel's finances? I am very curious about what it is like. It is said that the decoration cost of each hotel is about 150,000, which is comparable to Atour, but obviously the quality is much better than Atour. I don’t know how long it will take for such a hotel to be established. If there are more hotels like this, there really will be no Atour. Duo, what happened? One last thing to mention, if a guest leaves the room temporarily without clicking "Leave", it will seem like the electricity will be on all the time. This is certainly good for the guest, but is the hotel really that luxurious? Can't you save some electricity?

Opposite the hotel is a shopping mall, Nanjing food stall green tea and other restaurants are very good, the hotel is a five-minute walk to the subway station, and half an hour's drive to the expressway to various scenic spots in the West Lake.
The hotel has a free breakfast until ten o'clock. The variety is very rich, and the elderly and children are very happy to eat. During the Spring Festival, the hotel delivered breakfast to the room, and even prepared for the children. It was really heartwarming to receive a handwritten New Year greeting letter from the housekeeper on the hotel floor.
Our family loves to drink water. The room is cleaned promptly and clean every day. Special thanks to Yana. The service attitude is super good, she is good at communicating and helping, and is very kind.
The surrounding environment of the hotel is quiet, and I strongly recommend everyone to come here to experience it.

name:A‍n‍o‍n‍y‍m‍o‍u‍s‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior Queen Room
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Other
info:3 Reviews
rating:2
posted:Posted July 23, 2023
msg:住這麼多家酒店以來第一次忍不住給差評。
定的高級大床房，住進房間後發現衞生間和浴室是落地窗且衹有一層白色透光的硬簾，並沒有其他能夠完全遮蔽的窗簾，雖窗户對面沒有十分臨近的建築物，但依然讓人感覺十分不安全侵犯私隱；本以為酒店統一硬件其它房間也是如此，僅住一晚想着就不給店家添麻煩了；但離店後不放心查看其他房型圖片發現豪華大床房就是有額外的遮光簾的（見最後一張圖）。
衞生間浴室居然區別對待不統一配備遮蔽性強的窗簾，一家標榜豪華型的酒店連這麼基礎的硬件配置都做不到，真是匪夷所思！不要説高級大床房不配擁有遮光簾，你出去任何一家哪怕快捷酒店，都不會給客人住透明簾浴室的房間。
另外，房間門不嚴密，隔音效果差，房間門下面縫隙大，晚上透光；馬桶圈有污漬；**宣傳裏住店送的果盤有套保鮮膜，實際上也沒有。
實在忍不住給差評，希望店家注意一下客人的私隱，不論外面能不能看到裏面，都應該給衞生間配備起碼的設施。

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Superior Queen Room
info:Stayed in March 2023
info:Business travelers
info:10 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted March 9, 2023
msg:照片就懶得拍了。本來不想評價的，但實在忍不住槽點有點多。
先説優點吧，環境衞生和服務都不錯的，硬件設施也挺好（但有槽點，後面説）。房間還準備了免費一次性蒸汽眼罩和水果，還有一封手寫信，值得表揚。
再來説槽點或者叫改進建議吧：
淋浴：哇塞！大部分五星級酒店都很難看到這麼奢華的淋浴系統。趕緊試一下，結果。。。對不起，水温起伏實在大，又有點頻繁啊，所以整個洗澡過程都在調水温。。。。
燈光：觸摸板開關，挺高級啊。。。對不起，所有燈光（浴室除外）衹能同開同關，分了幾個主題，但也沒啥意思。最奇葩的是床頭左右2個大吊燈不能單獨控制。如果你想開着燈看電視，電視上印着2個大燈泡你基本是看不清啥。。。
空調：面板看着能調模式温度啥的，其實就是個擺設啊。空調師傅説中央空調你衹能控制開或者關。。。好吧，難怪我關了窗户開着空調製冷結果半夜12點熱醒了，穿短褲沒蓋被子那種。。。
早餐：一言難盡，屬於那種看上去東西不少（其實也不算多），真要挑起來發現沒啥好吃的。。。可能我太挑剔吧。但是，你喝果汁牛奶飲料衹提供一次性紙杯，連個玻璃杯都沒有的，是準備向如家看齊嗎？
好吧，説了這麼多並沒有要詆譭的意思。寫評價這會正好酒店打電話來問住店感受了，説明店家是真心想提高服務水平和質量的。有點像一個非常努力學習，刻苦用功的孩子，但無奈沒找到正確的學習方法，使勁使不到點子上，成績始終不理想。希望店家能理解我的意思。當然，這些都衹是我個人感受，可能比較挑剔，請多包涵。
----------------------------------------
